TIRE SYSTEMS INC./GROUP DISCOUNT WHOLESALERS
Group Discount Purchase Plan For
Stanford Students I Alumni • Faculty • Staff
Present a special wholesale warehouse group discount purchasing plan available only to rep
resentative* of participating groups, and offers up to a 50% discount or even more on the
TSI suggested list price of quality new tires, plus wholesale prices on the purchase of automo
tive batteries, shock absorbers and other products as they become available.
TSI passes savings on to you through volume buying, and encourages you to shop
around and compare. Mastercharge and Bankamericard welcome, or take advantage of financ
ing through your credit union. Remember, quality is never compromised for price, as only Ist
line or premium* quality new tires are considered by TSI.
The finest of quality together with the lowest of prices means that Tire Systems Inc.,.
is the ultimate in savings, convenience, satisfaction, and safe, happy motoring.

Group Discount Purchase Plan For
Stanford Students I Alumni • Faculty • Staff
Present a special wholesale warehouse group discount purchasing plan available only to rep
resentative* of participating groups, and offers up to a 50% discount or even more on the
TSI suggested list price of quality new tires, plus wholesale prices on the purchase of automo
tive batteries, shock absorbers and other products as they become available.
TSI passes savings on to you through volume buying, and encourages you to shop
around and compare. Mastercharge and Bankamericard welcome, or take advantage of financ
ing through your credit union. Remember, quality is never compromised for price, as only Ist
line or premium* quality new tires are considered by TSI.
The finest of quality together with the lowest of prices means that Tire Systems Inc.,.
is the ultimate in savings, convenience, satisfaction, and safe, happy motoring.

Group Discount Purchase Plan For
Stanford Students I Alumni • Faculty • Staff
Present a special wholesale warehouse group discount purchasing plan available only to rep
resentative* of participating groups, and offers up to a 50% discount or even more on the
TSI suggested list price of quality new tires, plus wholesale prices on the purchase of automo
tive batteries, shock absorbers and other products as they become available.
TSI passes savings on to you through volume buying, and encourages you to shop
around and compare. Mastercharge and Bankamericard welcome, or take advantage of financ
ing through your credit union. Remember, quality is never compromised for price, as only Ist
line or premium* quality new tires are considered by TSI.
The finest of quality together with the lowest of prices means that Tire Systems Inc.,.
is the ultimate in savings, convenience, satisfaction, and safe, happy motoring.

TIRE SYSTEMS INC./GROUP DISCOUNT WHOLESALERS
Group Discount Purchase Plan For
Stanford Students I Alumni • Faculty • Staff
Present a special wholesale warehouse group discount purchasing plan available only to rep
resentative* of participating groups, and offers up to a 50% discount or even more on the
TSI suggested list price of quality new tires, plus wholesale prices on the purchase of automo
tive batteries, shock absorbers and other products as they become available.
TSI passes savings on to you through volume buying, and encourages you to shop
around and compare. Mastercharge and Bankamericard welcome, or take advantage of financ
ing through your credit union. Remember, quality is never compromised for price, as only Ist
line or premium* quality new tires are considered by TSI.
The finest of quality together with the lowest of prices means that Tire Systems Inc.,.
is the ultimate in savings, convenience, satisfaction, and safe, happy motoring.

Group Discount Purchase Plan For
Stanford Students I Alumni • Faculty • Staff
Present a special wholesale warehouse group discount purchasing plan available only to rep
resentative* of participating groups, and offers up to a 50% discount or even more on the
TSI suggested list price of quality new tires, plus wholesale prices on the purchase of automo
tive batteries, shock absorbers and other products as they become available.
TSI passes savings on to you through volume buying, and encourages you to shop
around and compare. Mastercharge and Bankamericard welcome, or take advantage of financ
ing through your credit union. Remember, quality is never compromised for price, as only Ist
line or premium* quality new tires are considered by TSI.
The finest of quality together with the lowest of prices means that Tire Systems Inc.,.
is the ultimate in savings, convenience, satisfaction, and safe, happy motoring.

Group Discount Purchase Plan For
Stanford Students I Alumni • Faculty • Staff
Present a special wholesale warehouse group discount purchasing plan available only to rep
resentative* of participating groups, and offers up to a 50% discount or even more on the
TSI suggested list price of quality new tires, plus wholesale prices on the purchase of automo
tive batteries, shock absorbers and other products as they become available.
TSI passes savings on to you through volume buying, and encourages you to shop
around and compare. Mastercharge and Bankamericard welcome, or take advantage of financ
ing through your credit union. Remember, quality is never compromised for price, as only Ist
line or premium* quality new tires are considered by TSI.
The finest of quality together with the lowest of prices means that Tire Systems Inc.,.
is the ultimate in savings, convenience, satisfaction, and safe, happy motoring.

Group Discount Purchase Plan For
Stanford Students I Alumni • Faculty • Staff
Present a special wholesale warehouse group discount purchasing plan available only to rep
resentative* of participating groups, and offers up to a 50% discount or even more on the
TSI suggested list price of quality new tires, plus wholesale prices on the purchase of automo
tive batteries, shock absorbers and other products as they become available.
TSI passes savings on to you through volume buying, and encourages you to shop
around and compare. Mastercharge and Bankamericard welcome, or take advantage of financ
ing through your credit union. Remember, quality is never compromised for price, as only Ist
line or premium* quality new tires are considered by TSI.
The finest of quality together with the lowest of prices means that Tire Systems Inc.,.
is the ultimate in savings, convenience, satisfaction, and safe, happy motoring.

TIRE SYSTEMS INC./GROUP DISCOUNT WHOLESALERS
Group Discount Purchase Plan For
Stanford Students I Alumni • Faculty • Staff
Present a special wholesale warehouse group discount purchasing plan available only to rep
resentative* of participating groups, and offers up to a 50% discount or even more on the
TSI suggested list price of quality new tires, plus wholesale prices on the purchase of automo
tive batteries, shock absorbers and other products as they become available.
TSI passes savings on to you through volume buying, and encourages you to shop
around and compare. Mastercharge and Bankamericard welcome, or take advantage of financ
ing through your credit union. Remember, quality is never compromised for price, as only Ist
line or premium* quality new tires are considered by TSI.
The finest of quality together with the lowest of prices means that Tire Systems Inc.,.
is the ultimate in savings, convenience, satisfaction, and safe, happy motoring.

Group Discount Purchase Plan For
Stanford Students I Alumni • Faculty • Staff
Present a special wholesale warehouse group discount purchasing plan available only to rep
resentative* of participating groups, and offers up to a 50% discount or even more on the
TSI suggested list price of quality new tires, plus wholesale prices on the purchase of automo
tive batteries, shock absorbers and other products as they become available.
TSI passes savings on to you through volume buying, and encourages you to shop
around and compare. Mastercharge and Bankamericard welcome, or take advantage of financ
ing through your credit union. Remember, quality is never compromised for price, as only Ist
line or premium* quality new tires are considered by TSI.
The finest of quality together with the lowest of prices means that Tire Systems Inc.,.
is the ultimate in savings, convenience, satisfaction, and safe, happy motoring.

Group Discount Purchase Plan For
Stanford Students I Alumni • Faculty • Staff
Present a special wholesale warehouse group discount purchasing plan available only to rep
resentative* of participating groups, and offers up to a 50% discount or even more on the
TSI suggested list price of quality new tires, plus wholesale prices on the purchase of automo
tive batteries, shock absorbers and other products as they become available.
TSI passes savings on to you through volume buying, and encourages you to shop
around and compare. Mastercharge and Bankamericard welcome, or take advantage of financ
ing through your credit union. Remember, quality is never compromised for price, as only Ist
line or premium* quality new tires are considered by TSI.
The finest of quality together with the lowest of prices means that Tire Systems Inc.,.
is the ultimate in savings, convenience, satisfaction, and safe, happy motoring.
